Gone Girl (2014) is a psychological thriller directed by David Fincher, based on Gillian Flynn’s novel. The film follows Nick Dunne (Ben Affleck), whose wife Amy Dunne (Rosamund Pike) mysteriously disappears on their fifth wedding anniversary. As the media and police investigate, Nick becomes the prime suspect, and shocking secrets about their marriage begin to surface. The movie brilliantly explores themes of manipulation, toxic relationships, media influence, and identity, with Amy revealed as a highly intelligent and calculating mastermind. Known for its dark tone, unexpected twists, and Rosamund Pike’s iconic performance, Gone Girl is considered one of the best modern psychological thriller&quot;. Gone Girl (2014) is a psychological thriller directed by David Fincher, based on Gillian Flynn’s novel. The film follows Nick Dunne (Ben Affleck), whose wife Amy Dunne (Rosamund Pike) mysteriously disappears on their fifth wedding anniversary. As the media and police investigate, Nick becomes the prime suspect, and shocking secrets about their marriage begin to surface. The movie brilliantly explores themes of manipulation, toxic relationships, media influence, and identity, with Amy revealed as a highly intelligent and calculating mastermind. Known for its dark tone, unexpected twists, and Rosamund Pike’s iconic performance, Gone Girl is considered one of the best modern psychological thriller&quot;.
